BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Section 1 4 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998, I , the undersigned, hereby de-
clare my determination as set out in the Schedule a ppended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of  Land Nos. 405, 409 and 410 of 
Block 01, contained in the Cadastral Map No. 520001, situated in the Village of Homagama within the Grama Niladhari Division of No. 
486F - Homagama South in the Divisional Secretary's  Division of Homagama, in the District of Colombo, i n the Province of Western, 
referred to in Notice No. 52/0014 calling for claim s to land parcels which was duly published in the G azette No. 1526/21 of 06th De-
cember, 2007 in terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998.
